news Rahul Gandhi PM Modi speech today Covid cases in India West Bengal elections Corona vaccination India Covid-19: India's total tally crosses 1.56 crore cases, more than 2,000 deaths in 24 hours TIMESOFINDIA.COM | Updated: Apr 21, 2021, 11:16 IST Covid-19 patients admitted for treatment in Covid care center at a banquet hall near LNJP Hospital, New Delhi. NEW DELHI: The single-day rise in new coronavirus infections inched closer to 3 lakh with more than 2,000 daily deaths, according to the Union health ministry data updated on Wednesday. A total of 2,95,041 fresh infections were registered in a span of 24 hours, pushing India's total tally of Covid-19 cases to 1,56,16,130 while the active cases crossed the 21-lakh mark, the data updated at 8 am showed. This is the fastest one million cases that India has added since the beginning of the pandemic in 2019. It took India only four days to take its total tally of Covid-19 cases from 14 to 15 million. With 2,95,041 fresh infections reported in the last 24 hours, India globally stands second in terms of the highest daily cases. The United States of America had added more than 3 lakh new cases to its tally on January 2. The death toll increased to 1,82,553 on Wednesday with a record of 2,023 daily fatalities reported in the last 24 hours, as per official figures. Registering a steady increase for the 42nd in a row, the active cases have increased to 21,57,538, comprising 13.82 per cent of the total infections, while the national Covid-19 recovery rate has dropped to 85.01 per cent. The number of people who have recuperated from the disease surged to 1,32,76,039, while the case fatality rate has further dropped to 1.17 per cent, the data stated. India's Covid-19 tally had crossed the 20-lakh mark on August 7, 30 lakh on August 23, 40 lakh on September 5 and 50 lakh on September 16. It went past 60 lakh on September 28, 70 lakh on October 11, crossed 80 lakh on October 29, 90 lakh on November 20 and surpassed the one-crore mark on December 19. India crossed the grim milestone of 1.50 crore on April 19. According to the Indian Council of Medical Research (ICMR), 27,10,53,392 samples have been tested up to April 20 with 16,39,357 samples being tested on Tuesday.
